When are our Soccer Predictions Posted?

Our soccer predictions for today are released a few days before the scheduled match. The earlier they release the betting odds the better. Many other factors can also influence when we post our 1X2 predictions, but we prefer sooner rather than later. All our predictions are fully researched for the results at the end of 90 minutes. Extra time, red cards and penalties are not taken into account when making predictions. Soccer is also known as football in many countries around the world such as in European countries. Therefore we also provide football predictions as it is the same sport as soccer, just a different name.

Football Tips

We provide you with different tips which include ht/ft, both teams to score and correct score among many more for football fixtures taking place today. We try and get our football tips out before the day of the game, so you should find our football predictions available on this page ahead of the day of the match. Full time football predictions for matches taking place today, consist of 1X2 football betting tips for each game. Our football and soccer tips and predictions are available during the week and weekends. We update our football tips daily so you never miss out on our free 1X2 predictions.

Football Betting Tips

What are football betting tips?

They are football bets that can be placed by selecting the result of the football match. Therefore, when making football predictions you must choose the 1X2 result of the football and soccer match between the two teams. Football betting tips are determined by whether teams win, lose or draw the football match at the end of 90 minutes. The 1X2 betting market is the most common and popular betting option when making football bets. The football tips for today are based on historical analysis our experts conduct to provide you with the best football and soccer predictions.
